[30;1m10 | [0m[35mrelative) and base64 encode and embed them in the HTML output.[0m

[30;1m134 | [0m[35m## Nesting[0m
[30;1m135 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m136 | [0m[35mGeneric blocks can be nested as long as the block fence differs in number of leading tokens. This is[0m
[30;1m137 | [0m[35mfenced code blocks work. The minimum requirement is that at least three tokens are used.[0m
[30;1m138 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m139 | [0m[35m```[0m
[30;1m140 | [0m[35m//// note | Some title[0m

[31m--[ [0m[34mMatch #[0m[33m420[0m[34m of [0m[33m611[0m[31m ]--[0m

[30;1m82 | [0m[35msed, more complicated, or just make the first line signature more confusing. These[0m
[30;1m83 | [0m[35moptions are per block specific use a YAML syntax. They must be part of the header, which means no ne[0m
[30;1m84 | [0m[35mblock declaration and the options or between individual options. The options also must be indented a[0m
[30;1m85 | [0m[35m[0m
